<div id="main">

<h1>Avatar: The Way of Water (2022)</h1>
<div id="poster">

      <div class="card-body">
		<h2>Synopsis</h2><p>Set more than a decade after the events of the first film, “Avatar: The Way of Water” begins to tell the story of the Sully family (Jake, Neytiri, and their kids), the trouble that follows them, the lengths they go to keep each other safe, the battles they fight to stay alive, and the tragedies they endure. 
<h2>Metrics</h2><p>

<h1><a href="/news/253850830-Weekend-predictions-John-Wick-shooting-for-75-million-plus-this-weekend">Weekend predictions: John Wick shooting for $75 million plus this weekend</a></h1>
<p style="font-size: 75%">March 24th, 2023</p><A HREF="https://www.the-numbers.com/news/253850830-Weekend-predictions-John-Wick-shooting-for-75-million-this-weekend">
<img src="https://www.the-numbers.com/images/movies/John-Wick-Chapter-4-(2023)-1-News.jpg" class="img-fluid" alt="John Wick: Chapter 4">
</A>
<P>
<a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/John-Wick-Chapter-4-(2023)">John Wick: Chapter 4</a> will continue the remarkable run for the <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movies/franchise/John-Wick#tab=summary"><i>John Wick</i> franchise</a> by earning more on opening weekend than <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/John-Wick-Chapter-3-Parabellum-(2019)#tab=summary">John Wick: Chapter 3—Parabellum</a>, just as that movie beat the opening weekend of <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/John-Wick-Chapter-Two#tab=summary">John Wick: Chapter Two</a>, which had a better opening weekend than the original <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/John-Wick#tab=summary">John Wick</a>. It’s a rare franchise that manages to grow business with each new release, and an even rarer one that gets better reviews with each outing. But this is one of them. Exactly how much it’ll make this weekend remains a little uncertain, but things are looking very, very good.
<a href="/news/253850830-Weekend-predictions-John-Wick-shooting-for-75-million-plus-this-weekend">More...</a>
<br clear="all"><h1><a href="/news/253700830-Weekend-predictions-40-million-on-the-cards-for-Creed-III">Weekend predictions: $40 million on the cards for Creed III</a></h1>
<p style="font-size: 75%">March 3rd, 2023</p><A HREF="https://www.the-numbers.com/news/253700830-Weekend-predictions-40-million-the-cards-for-Creed-III">
<img src="https://www.the-numbers.com/images/movies/Creed-III-(2023)-1-News.jpg" class="img-fluid" alt="Creed III">
</A>
<P>
<a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Creed-III-(2023)#tab=summary">Creed III</a> looks likely to have the best opening weekend for a film in the <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movies/franchise/Creed">Creed</a> franchise</a>, which (not adjusted for inflation) would also give it the best opening for a <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movies/franchise/Rocky#tab=summary">Rocky movie</a> too, at least based on its excellent $5.45 million in previews, and our model’s expectations. <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Operation-Fortune-Ruse-de-guerre-(2022)#tab=summary">Operation Fortune: Ruse de guerre</a> looks like an also-ran, unfortunately. Meanwhile, <i>Ant-Man</i> and <i>Cocaine Bear</i> keep things interesting as our model picks apart this weekend’s box office prospects.
<a href="/news/253700830-Weekend-predictions-40-million-on-the-cards-for-Creed-III">More...</a>
<br clear="all"><h1><a href="/news/253550830-Weekend-predictions-Magic-Mike-could-still-win-weekend-from-1-550-theaters">Weekend predictions: Magic Mike could still win weekend from 1,550 theaters</a></h1>
<p style="font-size: 75%">February 10th, 2023</p><A HREF="https://www.the-numbers.com/news/253550830-Weekend-predictions-Magic-Mike-could-still-win-weekend-from-1-550-theaters">
<img src="https://www.the-numbers.com/images/movies/Magic-Mikes-Last-Dance-(2023)-1-News.jpg" class="img-fluid" alt="Magic Mike’s Last Dance">
</A>
<P>
<a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Magic-Mikes-Last-Dance-(2023)">Magic Mike’s Last Dance</a> launches in a modest 1,550 theaters this weekend—<a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/market/distributor/Warner-Bros">Warner Bros.</a> have not announced a precise figure—but that might be enough for it to pull off a win at the box office. Several films are in with a shot though, including <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Avatar-The-Way-of-Water-(2022)#tab=summary">Avatar: The Way of Water</a>, the re-release of <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Titanic-(1997)#tab=summary">Titanic</a>, and maybe even <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/80-for-Brady-(2023)#tab=summary">80 for Brady</a>, which has been perched at the top of the daily chart since last Sunday.

<br clear="all"><h1><a href="/news/253520830-Weekend-predictions-a-tight-race-at-the-top">Weekend predictions: a tight race at the top</a></h1>
<p style="font-size: 75%">February 3rd, 2023</p><A HREF="https://www.the-numbers.com/news/253520830-Weekend-predictions-a-tight-race-at-the-top">
<img src="https://www.the-numbers.com/images/movies/80-for-Brady-(2023)-1-News.jpg" class="img-fluid" alt="80 for Brady">
</A>
<P>
Three films have a realistic shot at topping the chart this weekend, with <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Knock-at-the-Cabin-(2023)#tab=summary">Knock at the Cabin</a> and <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/80-for-Brady-(2023)#tab=summary">80 for Brady</a> opening, and <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Avatar-The-Way-of-Water-(2022)#tab=summary">Avatar: The Way of Water</a> continuing to be, well, <i>Avatar</i>. With the likes of <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Chosen-The-Season-3-Finale-(2023)#tab=summary">The Chosen Season 3 Finale</a> ratcheting up good numbers already, we’re in for an interesting weekend at the box office.

<br clear="all"><h1><a href="/news/253480830-Weekend-predictions-will-Avatar-get-an-Oscar-boost-Can-Infinity-Pool-or-Left-Behind-break-through">Weekend predictions: will Avatar get an Oscar boost? Can Infinity Pool or Left Behind break through?</a></h1>
<p style="font-size: 75%">January 27th, 2023</p><A HREF="https://www.the-numbers.com/news/253480830-Weekend-predictions-will-Avatar-get-an-Oscar-boost-Can-Infinity-Pool-or-Left-Behind-break-through">
<img src="https://www.the-numbers.com/images/movies/Infinity-Pool-(2022-Canada)-1-News.jpg" class="img-fluid" alt="Infinity Pool">
</A>
<P>
The box office performance of <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Avatar-The-Way-of-Water-(2022)#tab=summary">Avatar: The Way of Water</a> certainly won’t be harmed this weekend by its 4 Oscar nominations (including Best Picture). How much it will help is the pertinent question for our weekend predictions. It’s the only film from last weekend’s top 10 that looks likely to get a bump from the nominations. One film that wasn’t in the top 10 last weekend could be revived by its Oscar noms: <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Fabelmans-The-(2022)">The Fabelmans</a> will add a thousand theaters and try to ride its seven nominations to the best weekend of its run so far. Other Oscar hopefuls expanding this weekend include <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Banshees-of-Inisherin-The-(2022)">The Banshees of Inisherin</a> (back in 1,205 theaters), <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Women-Talking-(2022)">Women Talking</a> (adding 553 locations to play in 707 theaters), <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Elvis-(2021)">Elvis</a> (rereleased in 841 theaters), and <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Tar-(2022)">Tár</a>, which expands from 106 to 537 movie theaters. Going up against all that are three new releases: <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Infinity-Pool-(2022-Canada)">Infinity Pool</a>, <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Left-Behind-Rise-of-the-Antichrist-(2022-Canada)#tab=summary">Left Behind: Rise of the Antichrist</a>, and <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Fear-(2023)">Fear</a>. That’s a lot of competition in the lower reaches of the top 10, but <i>Avatar</i> is in little danger of losing its top spot.
<a href="/news/253480830-Weekend-predictions-will-Avatar-get-an-Oscar-boost-Can-Infinity-Pool-or-Left-Behind-break-through">More...</a>

<P>
<a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Avatar-The-Way-of-Water-(2022)#tab=summary">Avatar: The Way of Water</a> is finally here. <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/person/23100401-James-Cameron">James Cameron</a>’s epic is expected to dominate at the box office well into the New Year and rack up hundreds of millions of dollars domestically (not to mention potentially billions worldwide) in the process. Exactly how many hundreds is the question, of course. Expectations for its opening weekend have been hovering around $150 million for quite a while, and ticked a little higher in the lead up to its release. Our final analysis points to around $170 million. But, as I’ll explain, that comes with a lot of caveats.

<br clear="all"><h1><a href="/news/253170830-Weekend-predictions-tis-the-weekend-before-Avatar-and-nothing-is-stirring">Weekend predictions: ’tis the weekend before Avatar, and nothing is stirring</a></h1>
<p style="font-size: 75%">December 9th, 2022</p><A HREF="https://www.the-numbers.com/news/253170830-Weekend-predictions-tis-the-weekend-before-Avatar-and-nothing-is-stirring">
<img src="https://www.the-numbers.com/images/movies/Violent-Night-(2022)-3-News.jpg" class="img-fluid" alt="Violent Night">
</A>
<P>
With holiday shopping in full swing, and <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Avatar-The-Way-of-Water-(2022)#tab=summary">Avatar: The Way of Water</a> arriving next week, movie theaters will be very quiet this weekend. Unless something unexpected happens, this will be the second-slowest weekend of the year, behind <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/box-office-chart/weekend/2022/01/28">the weekend of January 28</a>, when <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Spider-Man-No-Way-Home-(2021)">Spider-Man: No Way Home</a> recorded its sixth weekend win with a modest $11 million. <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Black-Panther-Wakanda-Forever-(2022)#tab=summary">Black Panther: Wakana Forever</a> is predicted to top the chart for a fifth time this weekend, with our model thinking it’ll earn about $13.5 million. If it can’t top $10 million (which is a possibility), this might prove to be the slowest weekend of the year.
<a href="/news/253170830-Weekend-predictions-tis-the-weekend-before-Avatar-and-nothing-is-stirring">More...</a>

<h2>Synopsis</h2><p>Set more than a decade after the events of the first film, “Avatar: The Way of Water” begins to tell the story of the Sully family (Jake, Neytiri, and their kids), the trouble that follows them, the lengths they go to keep each other safe, the battles they fight to stay alive, and the tragedies they endure.

<h1><a href="/news/253850830-Weekend-predictions-John-Wick-shooting-for-75-million-plus-this-weekend">Weekend predictions: John Wick shooting for $75 million plus this weekend</a></h1>
<p style="font-size: 75%">March 24th, 2023</p><A HREF="https://www.the-numbers.com/news/253850830-Weekend-predictions-John-Wick-shooting-for-75-million-this-weekend">
<img src="https://www.the-numbers.com/images/movies/John-Wick-Chapter-4-(2023)-1-News.jpg" class="img-fluid" alt="John Wick: Chapter 4">
</A>
<P>
<a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/John-Wick-Chapter-4-(2023)">John Wick: Chapter 4</a> will continue the remarkable run for the <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movies/franchise/John-Wick#tab=summary"><i>John Wick</i> franchise</a> by earning more on opening weekend than <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/John-Wick-Chapter-3-Parabellum-(2019)#tab=summary">John Wick: Chapter 3—Parabellum</a>, just as that movie beat the opening weekend of <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/John-Wick-Chapter-Two#tab=summary">John Wick: Chapter Two</a>, which had a better opening weekend than the original <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/John-Wick#tab=summary">John Wick</a>. It’s a rare franchise that manages to grow business with each new release, and an even rarer one that gets better reviews with each outing. But this is one of them. Exactly how much it’ll make this weekend remains a little uncertain, but things are looking very, very good.
<a href="/news/253850830-Weekend-predictions-John-Wick-shooting-for-75-million-plus-this-weekend">More...</a>
<br clear="all"><h1><a href="/news/253700830-Weekend-predictions-40-million-on-the-cards-for-Creed-III">Weekend predictions: $40 million on the cards for Creed III</a></h1>
<p style="font-size: 75%">March 3rd, 2023</p><A HREF="https://www.the-numbers.com/news/253700830-Weekend-predictions-40-million-the-cards-for-Creed-III">
<img src="https://www.the-numbers.com/images/movies/Creed-III-(2023)-1-News.jpg" class="img-fluid" alt="Creed III">
</A>
<P>
<a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Creed-III-(2023)#tab=summary">Creed III</a> looks likely to have the best opening weekend for a film in the <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movies/franchise/Creed">Creed</a> franchise</a>, which (not adjusted for inflation) would also give it the best opening for a <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movies/franchise/Rocky#tab=summary">Rocky movie</a> too, at least based on its excellent $5.45 million in previews, and our model’s expectations. <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Operation-Fortune-Ruse-de-guerre-(2022)#tab=summary">Operation Fortune: Ruse de guerre</a> looks like an also-ran, unfortunately. Meanwhile, <i>Ant-Man</i> and <i>Cocaine Bear</i> keep things interesting as our model picks apart this weekend’s box office prospects.
<a href="/news/253700830-Weekend-predictions-40-million-on-the-cards-for-Creed-III">More...</a>
<br clear="all"><h1><a href="/news/253550830-Weekend-predictions-Magic-Mike-could-still-win-weekend-from-1-550-theaters">Weekend predictions: Magic Mike could still win weekend from 1,550 theaters</a></h1>
<p style="font-size: 75%">February 10th, 2023</p><A HREF="https://www.the-numbers.com/news/253550830-Weekend-predictions-Magic-Mike-could-still-win-weekend-from-1-550-theaters">
<img src="https://www.the-numbers.com/images/movies/Magic-Mikes-Last-Dance-(2023)-1-News.jpg" class="img-fluid" alt="Magic Mike’s Last Dance">
</A>
<P>
<a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Magic-Mikes-Last-Dance-(2023)">Magic Mike’s Last Dance</a> launches in a modest 1,550 theaters this weekend—<a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/market/distributor/Warner-Bros">Warner Bros.</a> have not announced a precise figure—but that might be enough for it to pull off a win at the box office. Several films are in with a shot though, including <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Avatar-The-Way-of-Water-(2022)#tab=summary">Avatar: The Way of Water</a>, the re-release of <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Titanic-(1997)#tab=summary">Titanic</a>, and maybe even <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/80-for-Brady-(2023)#tab=summary">80 for Brady</a>, which has been perched at the top of the daily chart since last Sunday.
<a href="/news/253550830-Weekend-predictions-Magic-Mike-could-still-win-weekend-from-1-550-theaters">More...</a>
<br clear="all"><h1><a href="/news/253520830-Weekend-predictions-a-tight-race-at-the-top">Weekend predictions: a tight race at the top</a></h1>
<p style="font-size: 75%">February 3rd, 2023</p><A HREF="https://www.the-numbers.com/news/253520830-Weekend-predictions-a-tight-race-at-the-top">
<img src="https://www.the-numbers.com/images/movies/80-for-Brady-(2023)-1-News.jpg" class="img-fluid" alt="80 for Brady">
</A>
<P>
Three films have a realistic shot at topping the chart this weekend, with <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Knock-at-the-Cabin-(2023)#tab=summary">Knock at the Cabin</a> and <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/80-for-Brady-(2023)#tab=summary">80 for Brady</a> opening, and <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Avatar-The-Way-of-Water-(2022)#tab=summary">Avatar: The Way of Water</a> continuing to be, well, <i>Avatar</i>. With the likes of <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Chosen-The-Season-3-Finale-(2023)#tab=summary">The Chosen Season 3 Finale</a> ratcheting up good numbers already, we’re in for an interesting weekend at the box office.
<a href="/news/253520830-Weekend-predictions-a-tight-race-at-the-top">More...</a>
<br clear="all"><h1><a href="/news/253480830-Weekend-predictions-will-Avatar-get-an-Oscar-boost-Can-Infinity-Pool-or-Left-Behind-break-through">Weekend predictions: will Avatar get an Oscar boost? Can Infinity Pool or Left Behind break through?</a></h1>
<p style="font-size: 75%">January 27th, 2023</p><A HREF="https://www.the-numbers.com/news/253480830-Weekend-predictions-will-Avatar-get-an-Oscar-boost-Can-Infinity-Pool-or-Left-Behind-break-through">
<img src="https://www.the-numbers.com/images/movies/Infinity-Pool-(2022-Canada)-1-News.jpg" class="img-fluid" alt="Infinity Pool">
</A>
<P>
The box office performance of <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Avatar-The-Way-of-Water-(2022)#tab=summary">Avatar: The Way of Water</a> certainly won’t be harmed this weekend by its 4 Oscar nominations (including Best Picture). How much it will help is the pertinent question for our weekend predictions. It’s the only film from last weekend’s top 10 that looks likely to get a bump from the nominations. One film that wasn’t in the top 10 last weekend could be revived by its Oscar noms: <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Fabelmans-The-(2022)">The Fabelmans</a> will add a thousand theaters and try to ride its seven nominations to the best weekend of its run so far. Other Oscar hopefuls expanding this weekend include <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Banshees-of-Inisherin-The-(2022)">The Banshees of Inisherin</a> (back in 1,205 theaters), <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Women-Talking-(2022)">Women Talking</a> (adding 553 locations to play in 707 theaters), <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Elvis-(2021)">Elvis</a> (rereleased in 841 theaters), and <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Tar-(2022)">Tár</a>, which expands from 106 to 537 movie theaters. Going up against all that are three new releases: <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Infinity-Pool-(2022-Canada)">Infinity Pool</a>, <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Left-Behind-Rise-of-the-Antichrist-(2022-Canada)#tab=summary">Left Behind: Rise of the Antichrist</a>, and <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Fear-(2023)">Fear</a>. That’s a lot of competition in the lower reaches of the top 10, but <i>Avatar</i> is in little danger of losing its top spot.
<a href="/news/253480830-Weekend-predictions-will-Avatar-get-an-Oscar-boost-Can-Infinity-Pool-or-Left-Behind-break-through">More...</a>
<br clear="all"><h1><a href="/news/253390830-Weekend-predictions-Avatar-should-keep-Plane-grounded-this-weekend">Weekend predictions: Avatar should keep Plane grounded this weekend</a></h1>
<p style="font-size: 75%">January 13th, 2023</p><A HREF="https://www.the-numbers.com/news/253390830-Weekend-predictions-Avatar-should-keep-Plane-grounded-this-weekend">
<img src="https://www.the-numbers.com/images/movies/Plane-(2023)-1-News.jpg" class="img-fluid" alt="Plane">
</A>
<P>
<a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Avatar-The-Way-of-Water-(2022)#tab=summary">Avatar: The Way of Water</a> will get competition from no less than five films that can claim to be opening or expanding wide this weekend. The most serious threat to its box office dominance comes from <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Plane-(2023)#tab=summary">Plane</a>, an action thriller starring <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/person/22060401-Gerard-Butler">Gerard Butler</a> and <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/person/650500401-Mike-Colter">Mike Colter</a>. But in many ways <i>Avatar</i> is continuing to compete against its predecessor for box office history. This looks like another weekend that it will win with ease against more mortal competition.
<a href="/news/253390830-Weekend-predictions-Avatar-should-keep-Plane-grounded-this-weekend">More...</a>
<br clear="all"><h1><a href="/news/253320830-Weekend-predictions-Avatar-headed-for-the-top-again">Weekend predictions: Avatar headed for the top again</a></h1>
<p style="font-size: 75%">January 6th, 2023</p><A HREF="https://www.the-numbers.com/news/253320830-Weekend-predictions-Avatar-headed-for-the-top-again">
<img src="https://www.the-numbers.com/images/movies/Avatar-The-Way-of-Water-(2022)-1-News.jpg" class="img-fluid" alt="Avatar: The Way of Water">
</A>
<P>
<a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Avatar-The-Way-of-Water-(2022)#tab=summary">Avatar: The Way of Water</a> will top the box office chart again this weekend, as its seemingly unstoppable run continues into the New Year. The big question is when it will start losing momentum, and this weekend is the first big test it has faced, partly because <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/M3GAN#tab=summary">M3GAN</a> is looking to get 2023 off to a good start. Here are our model’s predictions going into the weekend…
<a href="/news/253320830-Weekend-predictions-Avatar-headed-for-the-top-again">More...</a>
<br clear="all"><h1><a href="/news/253280830-Weekend-predictions-61-5-million-is-the-target-for-Avatar-over-the-Holiday-weekend">Weekend predictions: $61.5 million is the target for Avatar over the Holiday weekend</a></h1>
<p style="font-size: 75%">December 23rd, 2022</p><A HREF="https://www.the-numbers.com/news/253280830-Weekend-predictions-61-5-million-is-the-target-for-Avatar-over-the-Holiday-weekend">
<img src="https://www.the-numbers.com/images/movies/Avatar-The-Way-of-Water-(2022)-4-News.jpg" class="img-fluid" alt="Avatar: The Way of Water">
</A>
<P>
A bevy of new films arrives in theaters for Christmas, but none are expected to put pressure on <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Avatar-The-Way-of-Water-(2022)#tab=summary">Avatar: The Way of Water</a> over the weekend. Here are our (abbreviated) predictions for the weekend…
<a href="/news/253280830-Weekend-predictions-61-5-million-is-the-target-for-Avatar-over-the-Holiday-weekend">More...</a>
<br clear="all"><h1><a href="/news/253230830-Weekend-predictions-Avatar-eyeing-170-million-opening">Weekend predictions: Avatar eyeing $170-million opening</a></h1>
<p style="font-size: 75%">December 16th, 2022</p><A HREF="https://www.the-numbers.com/news/253230830-Weekend-predictions-Avatar-eyeing-170-million-opening">
<img src="https://www.the-numbers.com/images/movies/Avatar-The-Way-of-Water-(2022)-1-News.jpg" class="img-fluid" alt="Avatar: The Way of Water">
</A>
<P>
<a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Avatar-The-Way-of-Water-(2022)#tab=summary">Avatar: The Way of Water</a> is finally here. <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/person/23100401-James-Cameron">James Cameron</a>’s epic is expected to dominate at the box office well into the New Year and rack up hundreds of millions of dollars domestically (not to mention potentially billions worldwide) in the process. Exactly how many hundreds is the question, of course. Expectations for its opening weekend have been hovering around $150 million for quite a while, and ticked a little higher in the lead up to its release. Our final analysis points to around $170 million. But, as I’ll explain, that comes with a lot of caveats.
<a href="/news/253230830-Weekend-predictions-Avatar-eyeing-170-million-opening">More...</a>
<br clear="all"><h1><a href="/news/253170830-Weekend-predictions-tis-the-weekend-before-Avatar-and-nothing-is-stirring">Weekend predictions: ’tis the weekend before Avatar, and nothing is stirring</a></h1>
<p style="font-size: 75%">December 9th, 2022</p><A HREF="https://www.the-numbers.com/news/253170830-Weekend-predictions-tis-the-weekend-before-Avatar-and-nothing-is-stirring">
<img src="https://www.the-numbers.com/images/movies/Violent-Night-(2022)-3-News.jpg" class="img-fluid" alt="Violent Night">
</A>
<P>
With holiday shopping in full swing, and <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Avatar-The-Way-of-Water-(2022)#tab=summary">Avatar: The Way of Water</a> arriving next week, movie theaters will be very quiet this weekend. Unless something unexpected happens, this will be the second-slowest weekend of the year, behind <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/box-office-chart/weekend/2022/01/28">the weekend of January 28</a>, when <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Spider-Man-No-Way-Home-(2021)">Spider-Man: No Way Home</a> recorded its sixth weekend win with a modest $11 million. <a href="https://www.the-numbers.com/movie/Black-Panther-Wakanda-Forever-(2022)#tab=summary">Black Panther: Wakana Forever</a> is predicted to top the chart for a fifth time this weekend, with our model thinking it’ll earn about $13.5 million. If it can’t top $10 million (which is a possibility), this might prove to be the slowest weekend of the year.
<a href="/news/253170830-Weekend-predictions-tis-the-weekend-before-Avatar-and-nothing-is-stirring">More...</a>

<h2>Daily Box Office Performance</h2>
<div id="box_office_chart">
<table >
